Frequent urination, straining to urinate & dribbling after passing urine are some signs of prostate disease. Look out for these.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Thyroid function is on the upper limit of normal. This may suggest an under functioning thyroid. The significance of this test can be better assessed by repeating the test. Vitamin D sufficient but suboptimal, Homocysteine level is within normal but above optimal.

Overview Notes: Sub Optimal vitamin D level - supplement with vitamin D as prescribed and then recheck your level in 3 to 4 months. Currently 32 but aim for between 50-80ng/ml.
Comment Key: CurrentComplaintRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Uric acid slightly raised likely due to red meat and alcohol intake. No gout at present.

Frequent urination, straining to urinate & dribbling after passing urine are some signs of prostate disease. Look out for these.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Sub Optimal vitamin D level - supplement with vitamin D as prescribed and then recheck your level in 3 to 4 months. Currently 32 but aim for between 50-80ng/ml.
Comment Key: MensHealthRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Uric acid slightly raised likely due to red meat and alcohol intake. No gout at present.

Overview Notes: Decrease alcohol intake to 14 units per week or less (equivalent to 10 small glasses of wine). Try to replace red meats with leaner protein.
Comment Key: VitalsNote
Comment Value: Normal measurements
Special Investigation Notes: Uric acid slightly raised likely due to red meat and alcohol intake. No gout at present.
